                                <div  class="rte"><div class="celwidget aplus-module 3p-module-b aplus-standard" data-csa-c-id="nooj0s-1z2fwo-vwb8pk-z2ud8l" data-cel-widget="aplus-3p-module-b">
<div class="aplus-module-wrapper aplus-3p-fixed-width"><img alt="15.6 portable monitor" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/S/aplus-media-library-service-media/65b4e5a6-3acc-418a-8ef6-faf370d42173.__CR0,0,970,600_PT0_SX970_V1___.jpeg" class="a-spacing-base" data-src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/S/aplus-media-library-service-media/65b4e5a6-3acc-418a-8ef6-faf370d42173.__CR0,0,970,600_PT0_SX970_V1___.jpeg" />
<h3 class="a-spacing-mini">Arzora portable 15.6 inch monitor</h3>
<p class="a-spacing-base">1920 x 1080 FHD 15.6 inch thin portable monitor: 1920 x 1080 FHD resolution, 0.2 inch thinnest thickness. Offer you a comfortable display of your home computer, improve your travel experience 16.7 million. Colour & 100% sRGB colour space: 100% sRGB colour coverage, 320 cd/m² brightness, 1200:1 contrast for finer details. Provide stunning pictures while playing, reading or working etc. Quick response: Use the latest technology to ensure a seamless gaming experience by reducing screen facts and tearing. Built-in 2 speakers: Built-in 2 speakers deliver incredible sound and more immersive entertainment, especially when you listen to music/watch movies/play games. Smart case: The smart case with magnetic function is made of PU leather, which provides excellent protection for the entire monitor, and can also be folded into different positions to create a stand.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="celwidget aplus-module 3p-module-b aplus-standard" data-csa-c-id="r1wnuf-8tc5fb-pmlo4b-h532zi" data-cel-widget="aplus-3p-module-b">
<div class="aplus-module-wrapper aplus-3p-fixed-width"><img alt="Business share screen" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/S/aplus-media-library-service-media/f08ece15-d219-4c29-b521-052ddab36e82.__CR0,0,970,600_PT0_SX970_V1___.jpg" class="a-spacing-base" data-src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/S/aplus-media-library-service-media/f08ece15-d219-4c29-b521-052ddab36e82.__CR0,0,970,600_PT0_SX970_V1___.jpg" />
<h3 class="a-spacing-mini">Tips:</h3>
<p class="a-spacing-base">This portable monitor does not contain a battery. The monitor should be adjusted when adjusting the brightness or similar. to flicker or restart, please check whether the power supply of the monitor is sufficient. It is recommended to use a power supply that supports 5V/2.4A or higher. If the Type-C port of your computer is not a Type-C port with full functionality, you can connect to the Type-C port or HDMI port. If your computer does not have a fully equipped Type-C port, please use HDMI to Mini HDMI to connect. If you want to connect your phone, please make sure that the Type-C port of your phone is a fully equipped Type-C port. If not, it would not work with the portable ARZOPA monitor.</p>
</div>
</div>
